Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

of PRINCE BLESSY on 14th April 2018
SUREKHA  B

Public Notices

surgery by Dr. R. Venkatesh, MS, MCH, The Best Hospital Private Limited, Old No. 9, New No. 22, Vellala Street, Kodambakkam, 
Chennai-600 024, (Reg-9492). By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as YAZHINI PAVAI. K
Pudukkottai,	
K. SARAVANAN
6th February 2020.

son of Thiru  A. Sriramulu on 14th June 2010 by way of Registered Deed No. 972/2010. Sub-Register Office, Thiruvottiyur, 
hereafter S. Janarthanan shall henceforth be known as J. JANARTHANAN.
Chennai,	
M. JAYALAKSHMI
7th February 2020.                                                                                                                                                 (Adoptive Mother)

Taluk, Sivagangai-630 202.

son on 9th May 1988 by way of registered deed bearing No. 25/1988 on the Sub-Register Office at Devakottai. My Adopted 
Father and Mother passed away on 8th July 2008 and 25th March 2013 respectively. Hereafter I shall henceforth be known 
as A. SOUNDARARAJAN.
Sivagangai,	
V. SOUNDARARAJAN
7th February 2020.
